  none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  padding:0in 3.0pt 0in 3.0pt;height:39.85pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:8.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
  color:black'>[1...1]</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=336 valign=top style='width:3.5in;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;
  padding:0in 3.0pt 0in 3.0pt;height:39.85pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
  color:black'>Question</span></b><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:
  "Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>: Is it useful to document service in
  foreign armed forces?</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
  color:black'>Answer</span></b><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
  color:black'>: No, not at this time. </span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
  color:black'>This concept is out-of-scope at this time. </span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:8.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><b><i><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
  color:black'> </span></i></b></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<h4><a name="BKM_CCBE5EDA_C9CA_456F_9D80_186017054BA4"><span style='color:#0F0F0F'>PayGradeCode
</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Defines the level of compensation for a position, normalized
across military branches. This value set harmonizes the concepts used in VA wit
those specified by FDA for Occupational Data for Health implementations.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>This specification will use the latest FDA value set specified in </span><a
href="#BKM_0D6D76FC_1E59_4574_B56F_1BD12F5BD18F"><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'> Job Supervisory Level or Pay </span></a><a
href="#BKM_0D6D76FC_1E59_4574_B56F_1BD12F5BD18F"><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Grade (ODH)</span></a><span style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>.  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h4><a name="BKM_E4F59E0A_7366_4ACB_94EB_E3D6CEB81063"><span style='color:#0F0F0F'>SeparationReasonCode
</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>&quot;Additional description for separation reason beyond
discharge status value.&quot;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Note: </span></b><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>This may need to be specified as a code value rather than a text
value.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Separation reason codes. These codes will be addressed as
gaps/change requests in SNOMED CT using the Solor Project:
https://logica.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SOLOR/pages/865271876/Military+Service+History+and+Status</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
color:black'>Requirements: </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:11.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><img border=0 width=474 height=1020 id="Picture 99"
src="image007.jpg"><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;color:black'>   </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><a name="BKM_46489E03_6B27_43CF_9945_9452CB1BAAB0"></a><a
name="IMPLEMENTATION_AND_TESTING_GUIDANCE_"><span style='color:#0F0F0F'>  </span> </a><a
name="_Toc57591056">Implementation and Testing Guidance</a>  </h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>The current VA API uses an ad-hoc verification operation and
allows third-party systems to to retrieve the military service - including
combat episodes. This track will demonstrate how this API can be provided using
a standards-based approach that includes FHIR resources and terminology
constraints using concepts from LOINC, SNOMED CT, and CDC ODH  - as specified
in the associated Logica project intended to validate the extensions needed to
represent Military Service and Combat Episodes using Observation resource
similar to ODH. The current REST API is used primarily verify veteran status
for benefits associated with military service (e.g., insurance coverage, discounts,
education assistance, etc.). The enhanced FHIR-based API will make this API
readily available for  health-related purposes: social determinants of health,
risk factors for specific conditions (e.g. health disease, major depressive
disorder, suicidal ideation). </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>In addition to proving the feasibility of FHIR resources to
provide equivalent capabilities to the current API, this project will also
introduce standards-based concepts in place of local VA terminology for
discharge status and separation reason as well we reusing CDC ODH concept to
represent the military branch and pay grade of a Veteran.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="BKM_91F9D1F5_7413_4A99_B13A_496057EF2A40"></a><a
name="TESTING_WORKFLOW"><span style='color:#0F0F0F'>  </span> </a><a
name="_Toc57591057">Testing Workflow</a> </h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>This workflow identifies  the activities and API calls required to
address the requirements specified in the </span><a
href="#BKM_AAE71534_C7E9_47A1_9421_6733DA4A8780"><span style='font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Use Case Analysis</span></a><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h5><a name="BKM_9C9D4137_00B3_4F4B_AAD1_0F8CA48F079C"><span style='color:#0F0F0F'>Testing
Workflow </span></a></h5>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>The following is a testing workflow for this API. Successful
testing may also use test scripts and pre-conditions to results of an EHR
invoking the proposed API to verify status and retrieve the military history
information of a Veteran using FHIR-based resources. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><a name="BKM_587CBB10_EA2D_440E_BBCC_394BE0D06C12"><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></a></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><img border=0
width=753 height=540 id="Picture 100"
src="image008.gif"></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Figure </span><span style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>7</span><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>: Testing Workflow</span></p>

<h3><a name="BKM_9E183C1C_CB88_4A77_B110_D6702CAAC30B"></a><a
name="VERIFY_VETERAN_STATUS__STEP_1"><span style='color:#0F0F0F'>  </span> </a><a
name="_Toc57591058">Verify Veteran Status: Step 1</a> </h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Scenario #1: Veteran Confirmation and Verification</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>A Veteran is receiving treatment in the community and invokes the
&quot;$veteranStatus&quot; operation using the Veteran's demographics (e.g.
fist, last, dob, ssn). If the Veteran is verified then the client application
proceed to Step 2.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Scenario Step 1 : Search the Patient resource to evaluate whether
&quot;Sam Share&quot; is a confirmed/validated Veteran based on the VA-specific
extension </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Action:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>HAPI FHIR Client Code - Use the following code snippet to execute
this action in your own client.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>// Create a client (only needed once)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>FhirContext ctx = new FhirContext();</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>IGenericClient client =
ctx.newRestfulGenericClient(&quot;http://hapi.fhir.org/baseR4&quot;);</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>// Invoke the client</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Bundle bundle = client.search().forResource(Patient.class)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.where(new
StringClientParam(&quot;family&quot;).matches().value(&quot;Share&quot;))</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.where(new
StringClientParam(&quot;given&quot;).matches().value(&quot;Sam&quot;))</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.where(new
TokenClientParam(&quot;identifier&quot;).exactly().systemAndCode(&quot;urn:oid:1.1.1.1.1&quot;,
&quot;1032702&quot;))</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.prettyPrint()</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.execute();</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Request    GET http://hapi.fhir.org/baseR4/Patient?family=Share&amp;given=Sam&amp;identifier=urn:oid:1.1.1.1.1|1032702&amp;_pretty=true</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Request Headers    </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Accept-Charset: utf-8</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Accept: application/fhir+xml;q=1.0, application/fhir+json;q=1.0,
application/xml+fhir;q=0.9, application/json+fhir;q=0.9</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>User-Agent: HAPI-FHIR/5.2.0-SNAPSHOT (FHIR Client; FHIR 4.0.1/R4;
apache)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Accept-Encoding: gzip</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Response    HTTP 200 OK</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Response Headers    </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>x-request-id: xeQWJ1xsJu7hZt4s</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>date: Thu, 10 Sep 2020 12:46:19 GMT</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>last-modified: Thu, 10 Sep 2020 12:46:19 GMT</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>server: nginx/1.14.0 (Ubuntu)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>transfer-encoding: chunked</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>x-powered-by: HAPI FHIR 5.2.0-SNAPSHOT REST Server (FHIR Server;
FHIR 4.0.1/R4)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>connection: keep-alive</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>content-type: application/fhir+json;charset=utf-8</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Result Body JSON bundle (4055 bytes)    </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Bundle contains 1 / 1 entries</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>    Patient/sam-share-ssgt-veteran/_history/1    12:33:05</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Raw Message</span></p>

color:black'>            &quot;code&quot;: &quot;2106-3&quot;,</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Success Criteria:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Examine the value of the extension: &quot;extension&quot;: [ {
&quot;url&quot;:
&quot;http://hl7.org/fhir/us/core/StructureDefinition/us-veteran-status&quot;,
&quot;valueCode&quot;: &quot;verified&quot; }, </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>If &quot;verified&quot; then proceed to step #2</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Bonus po</span><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>int:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
color:black'>  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h3><a name="BKM_14DAAADB_4B6A_4950_BEFE_ABBC1B4544AB"></a><a
name="SEARCH_MILITARY_SERVICE_HISTORY__STEP_2"><span style='color:#0F0F0F'>  </span> </a><a
name="_Toc57591059">Search Military Service History: Step 2</a> </h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Scenario Step 2: Search the Observation resource for a list of
Military Service Episodes: search by &quot;subject&quot; (i.e. Patient/Veteran)
and by  &quot;patient&quot; and &quot;code&quot; search parameters</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Action:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Client Code - Use the following code snippet to execute this
action in your own client.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>// Create a client (only needed once)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>FhirContext ctx = new FhirContext();</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>IGenericClient client =
ctx.newRestfulGenericClient(&quot;http://hapi.fhir.org/baseR4&quot;);</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>// Invoke the client</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>Bundle bundle = client.search().forResource(Observation.class)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.where(new
TokenClientParam(&quot;code&quot;).exactly().code(&quot;bdb89d1f-f2c1-497b-ad7e-9ab8078a124b&quot;))</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.where(new
ReferenceClientParam(&quot;patient&quot;).hasId(&quot;sam-share-ssgt-veteran&quot;))</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.prettyPrint()</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>.execute();</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:10.0pt;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>
